    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

  <span id="freeText12561017165724508711" style="display:none">Five months ago, Camryn and Andrew, both dealing with personal hardships, met on a Greyhound bus. They fell in love and proved that when two people are meant to be together, fate will find a way to make it happen.<br /><br />Now, in the highly anticipated sequel to <em>The Edge of Never</em>, Camryn and Andrew are pursuing their love for music and living life to the fullest as they always swore to do. But when tragedy befalls them, their relationship is put to the ultimate test. As Camryn tries to numb her pain, Andrew makes a bold decision: To get their life back on track, they'll set out on another cross-country road trip. Together they find excitement, passion, adventure-and challenges they never could have anticipated.</span>

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17374029-the-edge-of-always">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer536231717" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17866772618984828583"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383620966i/6613839._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>** FULL SPOILER FREE REVIEW NOW POSTED ** <br/><br/><b><i>The Edge of Always</i>  perfectly recaptured that special "feeling" from the first book, stayed true to the characters and told a beautiful story filled with romance, adventure and emotional depth. It also fully brought Andrew and Camryn's journey full circle giving a wonderful sense of closure to their story. </b><br/><br/>I have to admit that I was very nervous about reading this book because I felt a certain apprehension at reading the sequel to a book that really coul</span>
  <span id="freeText17866772618984828583" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383620966i/6613839._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>** FULL SPOILER FREE REVIEW NOW POSTED ** <br><br><b><i>The Edge of Always</i>  perfectly recaptured that special "feeling" from the first book, stayed true to the characters and told a beautiful story filled with romance, adventure and emotional depth. It also fully brought Andrew and Camryn's journey full circle giving a wonderful sense of closure to their story. </b><br><br>I have to admit that I was very nervous about reading this book because I felt a certain apprehension at reading the sequel to a book that really could have been a standalone. <i>The Edge of Never </i>was truly one of my most favorite books of 2012 and it ended in such a beautiful way that I was completely happy with the story and a little worried to read more because I didn't want these characters I'd come to love so dearly to be put through any unnecessary drama. Well, turns out I had no reason to fear! J.A. Redmerski did a wonderful job of writing a sequel that did true justice to characters we'd all grown so fond of.<br><br>Please note that this is not a standalone and should only be read after <i>The Edge of Never</i>. It is a direct continuation that follows the same main couple, Andrew and Camryn, and the story is told from both their POVs in alternating chapters giving us a very well-rounded view of the whole story.<br><br>Right from the beginning of the book, I slipped right back into their story as though I'd never left. Even though I did not have time to reread book #1 first, I still was able to reconnect instantly. I could feel the depths of their well-deserved happiness and couldn't help but to be caught up in the moment. After everything they'd been through, they needed this. But the blurb hinted at a tragedy and so there was a constant tension in the background of the blissful setting as I dreaded the inevitable devastation that I knew was coming. And I won't lie that when it hit, it hurt like <em>hell</em>.<br><br>But Andrew and Camryn had already been through a lot together and the foundation of their relationship was solid and binding. I never had any doubt that they'd get through it no matter how bad it got... and they did. But it wasn't an easy journey. Weighed down by their loss, Camryn began to fall apart and out of his love for her, Andrew came up with a plan to help her heal... he took them back on the road. And through their journey they slowly began heal the broken pieces of their hearts and find their happiness once again.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"This is our life. We met on the road; we grew to know and to love each other on the road. It's where we were meant to be for however long, and what we're going to do until it becomes clear we were meant to do something else."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Andrew Parrish just made me melt and swoon over and over again. The depths of his love for Camryn just rolled off the page and I loved how he was willing to go to any lengths to ensure her happiness.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"You're the world to me," I whisper onto her lips. "I hope you never forget that."</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>"I'll never forget," she whispers back… "But if I ever do, for whatever reason, I hope you'll always find a way to remind me."</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>… "Always."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Along the road, Andrew also helped Cam get closure for things from her past that were still hurting her and that she hadn't yet dealt with. I swear that man was just a saint. He was the perfect blend of just a regular, tender, loving guy and a hot, dominant Alpha. I absolutely adored him!!<br><br>But I loved that Cam helped him too. It went both ways and honestly, they both healed each other by finding moments of happiness each day and living every minute of their time together to it's absolutely fullest. Some minutes made me tear up, others made me laugh hysterically. Along the road memories were created, promises were made and a life was rebuilt.<br><br>Andrew and Cam's journey was unlike any other I've read. Their story really stands out and I was just so impressed with the direction the author took this story in and with the way she stayed so true to these beloved characters. This series has the perfect blend of romance and adventure combined with heartfelt emotional depth. I think fans of <em>The Edge of Never </em>will be very happy with this sequel!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"We're in it together. All of it. Do you believe that?"<br>She nods. "Yes."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><br>4.5 stars<br><br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="17866772618984828583" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

It's where we were meant to be for however long and it's what we're going to do until it becomes clear that we were meant to do something else."</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384425600ra/6874352.gif' width='400' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>When we are kids we have dreams. Or seeing the world. Of singing in front of a crowd. Of finding the other half of our souls. Life has a way to fulfill your dreams and take them away unexpectedly. Only by believing and keep </span>
  <span id="freeText16189239058177273652" style="display:none"><b>3 Our Life, on the Road Stars<br><br><i>"Because this is our life. We met on the road; we grew up to know and to love each other on the road. It's where we were meant to be for however long and it's what we're going to do until it becomes clear that we were meant to do something else."</i></b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384425600ra/6874352.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>When we are kids we have dreams. Or seeing the world. Of singing in front of a crowd. Of finding the other half of our souls. Life has a way to fulfill your dreams and take them away unexpectedly. Only by believing and keep dreaming you can make the most and live your life that you have always wanted.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384425600ra/6874353.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Camryn &amp; Andrew</b>, 2 kids, have suffered, have dreamt, have conquered their fears and overcome death to be together. Two lost souls that met by chance and fell in love by fate after the heart-pounding and deeply romantic <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17870258.The_Edge_of_Never" title="The Edge of Never by J.A. Redmerski" rel="nofollow noopener">The Edge of Never</a>, are together and they have many difficult decisions to take. About family, responsibilities and choosing between their dreams. Always together and in love.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384425600ra/6874354.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Deeply, romantic and passionate as only a young couple can be, full of hope and despair as only life can mingle them. This book lacked the intensity of the first and it actually became a chronicle. A family saga and moments in a life that Camryn and Andrew tried and succeed to make the most of it. <br><br>While I liked it and I was thrilled to read this book, somehow my expectations overwhelmed me and I couldn't loved it. The twist was obvious miles away as was the resolution and the climax. Drawn out scenes, over-explaining and unnecessary drama. A shorter story with some dramatic notes would have suited me better. Though I can't complain the way this book ended...<br><br><i>
  <b>"Our story us over, yes, but our journey isn't, because we'll always live on the edge until the day we die."</b>
</i><br><br><i>and even then...</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384425600ra/6874355.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>Pre-release meltdown</i><br><b>My day was pretty much uneventful..</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409647ra/802198.gif" width="320" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then......<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/592655.gif" width="500" height="288" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>The Edge of Always (The Edge of Never, #2)<br>by J.A. Redmerski<br>This is the sequel to the bestselling novel, THE EDGE OF NEVER.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380331803ra/692736.gif" width="300" height="146" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/296985.gif" width="320" height="289" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/443183.gif" width="500" height="282" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>Just...     <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_686235116" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/686235116" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/686235116?book_show_action=true">Aug 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17374029-the-edge-of-always">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=netgalley-edelweiss">netgalley-edelweiss</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=new-adult-express">new-adult-express</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=read-to-review">read-to-review</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer686235116" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7268805331634955128"><b> 3 BANG-MY-HEAD-ON-THE-WALL STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435912ra/880866.gif' width='300' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>The Edge of Never was one of the VERY first New Adult books I read. It helped kickstart my fascination with this genre and had one of the most unique, inspirational, and heartwarming storylines I’d ever read. After finishing the first book, I was in a warm, content, fuzzy place where I was satisfied to let go of these characters. That being said, though, another book about them is cool too!<br/><br/>That is, until the second book turned out to be a disappointment.<br/><br/>For one,</span>
  <span id="freeText7268805331634955128" style="display:none"><b> 3 BANG-MY-HEAD-ON-THE-WALL STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435912ra/880866.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The Edge of Never was one of the VERY first New Adult books I read. It helped kickstart my fascination with this genre and had one of the most unique, inspirational, and heartwarming storylines I’d ever read. After finishing the first book, I was in a warm, content, fuzzy place where I was satisfied to let go of these characters. That being said, though, another book about them is cool too!<br><br>That is, until the second book turned out to be a disappointment.<br><br>For one, the plot just fell flat. I mean, below ground zero flat. I could understand if the beginning of the book started out slow, but I expect it to build up or change a bit. Which it didn’t. I was literally waiting for something <b>
  <i>epic</i>
</b> or something that would have shook me out of my bored stupor. Something did happen, of course. It was that “tragedy” in the blurb. <br><br>Okay. I do not want to sound like I’m a conceited, unemotional, uncaring bitch, but that “tragedy?” <b>Did.Not.Affect.Me.At.All. Whatsoever.</b> Maybe because you have to live it to experience it? I know <b>for sure</b> a few of my GR friends will be emotionally invested in this story because of said tragedy, and that’s totally normal. But for me, I’m going to attribute my lack of response to the <i>very</i> slow plot buildup, then – SMACK – you get this plot twist that is entirely predictable and not very impressive. <br><br>So. As a result of that tragedy, Camryn just spirals downhill and crashes. And OMG. Did I want to smack her in the face because of the choices she made!!! At this part, I feel like the author overexaggerated her grief and downgraded Andrew’s emotions. Flippety-flop. Both on rather extreme ends. <br><br>Next. Andrew wants to spice up their lives because Camryn acts like a dead person and he’s <s>not regularly getting laid</s> worried about her state of health and their relationship. They go on this road trip, which isn’t a bad idea!! But! Did the author have to add in so many time gaps!!!!!!!!!!! I’m not even joking here. One page, they’ll be celebrating Camryn’s birthday in December and the next page flips to late January (okay not a big gap, but still what happened to the days in-between?). I can accept that, as long as there aren’t more of those gaps. BUT NO. After January, guess where it goes? TO MAY. Like, do they need a calendar or something? I want to know what the heck they did in February, March, and April for goodness sake. After that one, everything goes normal for a while until the ending and I’ll get to that part later. <br><br>Next. This one particular event around 55% into the book DROVE.ME.INSANE. No spoilers here. For one, the author just shouldn’t have added it into the book. It cut the flow. It didn’t go with the story. It almost seemed as if she added this in just to introduce Bray and Elias (starring in the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18189342.Song_of_the_Fireflies" title="Song of the Fireflies by J.A. Redmerski" rel="nofollow noopener">Song of the Fireflies</a>) and not as part of the plot. Quick zip-in and out. I still cannot believe she would do this to her characters. It was completely unnecessary. Andrew and Camryn even agreed to just drop it so what the heck was the point of adding it in besides creating unnecessary drama? Afterwards, no mention of this scene, hence my notion of her adding this to just quickly introduce Bray and Elias. Oh btw, I absolutely <b>
  <i>abhor</i>
</b> the idea of anyone else touching Andrew besides Camryn and though there is no form of cheating going on, I wanted to punch out his nuts regardless. Even though he’s “innocent.” <br><br>Next. The believability of the story. So they take this <b>
  <i>very long</i>
</b> road trip and when they get back, they’re already planning on their future trips. And I’m not talking about state-to-state in the US, this is full-on flying to Africa, Europe, South America, etc. I get that Andrew has this handy dandy trust fund and they make good money from their gigs, but seriously?! To me, this just sounds so very impractical and unbelievable. What if they have a family? Eventually, how are they going to be strapping a baby or two on one of these tours? <br><br>Huh. Maybe that’s why <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ the author jumped right from present day Camryn and Andrew to <b><i>fifteen years later</i></b> where the kid grew up.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> =_=<br><br>^^ That was one of the major time gaps I had a problem with. Right before this one, it goes from June to “many months later” to next February to fifteen years later. I got this feeling the author rushed to finish the story and slapped on an epilogue for good measure.<br><br>All this being said though, there were traces of <b>EPIC</b> scenes scattered throughout the book, and these alone helped me power through (or I would have DNF’ed it). There were two memorable scenes (especially the one where Camryn and Andrew are in separate hotel rooms) that truly touched me. Made me <b>
  <i>cry</i>
</b>. Made me <b>
  <i>connect</i>
</b> with the characters. Made me <b>
  <i>feel</i>
</b> something. <b>THAT</b> is what I want to see throughout the book, not just in ounces placed in rare locations. <b>THAT</b> is what this author is famous for, and what I expected when I read this book. <br><br>Overall, the story makes a solid 3. It bored me to tears at times, and the characters frustrated the heck out of me. The time gaps were a big no-no. Not a bad book by any means, but fell flat of expectations that are usually attached to a second book in a series, particularly this one. <br><br><i>ARC provided by publisher via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><b>For more reviews, freebie lists, &amp; giveaways visit my blog!</b><br><a href="http://bookvigilantereviews.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16648163120976004154"><b>4 ♥ ♥ ♥ Andrew Parrish ♥ ♥ ♥ Stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/b98edc04-4c56-447a-baaf-77528398e5a2_zps45282c75.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><i>
  <blockquote>When everything falls apart, love remains...</blockquote>
</i><br/>Camryn and Andrew are together. Happy. More in love than they’ve ever been. Then something big happens to them both. Something that changes their lives forever. Camryn starts to change in little ways. Andrew knows he was to do something to bring her back to herself. He decides they need to go back to the start. Back on the road.<br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/0d6e141d-c635-4ab8-8f54-51314fc44079_zpsae8c3a99.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>Andrew Parrish. Andrew will always have a special place in my heart. I fell i</span>
  <span id="freeText16648163120976004154" style="display:none"><b>4 ♥ ♥ ♥ Andrew Parrish ♥ ♥ ♥ Stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/b98edc04-4c56-447a-baaf-77528398e5a2_zps45282c75.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384092341i/6770294.jpg" alt=" photo b98edc04-4c56-447a-baaf-77528398e5a2_zps45282c75.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>When everything falls apart, love remains...</blockquote>
</i><br>Camryn and Andrew are together. Happy. More in love than they’ve ever been. Then something big happens to them both. Something that changes their lives forever. Camryn starts to change in little ways. Andrew knows he was to do something to bring her back to herself. He decides they need to go back to the start. Back on the road.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/0d6e141d-c635-4ab8-8f54-51314fc44079_zpsae8c3a99.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384177633i/6803894.jpg" alt=" photo 0d6e141d-c635-4ab8-8f54-51314fc44079_zpsae8c3a99.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Andrew Parrish. Andrew will always have a special place in my heart. I fell in love with him even more in this story. He is funny, sweet, loving, sexy, and will make you swoon like no other!<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/b25ceba6-3d04-48f2-8f7a-6f86ab4ffd0a_zpsda683bb3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384177633i/6803895.jpg" alt=" photo b25ceba6-3d04-48f2-8f7a-6f86ab4ffd0a_zpsda683bb3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>‘I promise to love you forever in this life and wherever we go in the afterlife, because I know I can’t go on in any life unless you’re in it too.’<br><br> ‘You’re the other half of me that I know I can never live without.’<br><br>‘Where else would I be than wherever you are?’</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/d397f5ea-f41c-4b5f-8786-a4f6042aeed2_zps22453eb0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384177633i/6803896.jpg" alt=" photo d397f5ea-f41c-4b5f-8786-a4f6042aeed2_zps22453eb0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There were many things I loved about this book. One of my favorite scenes- when they went back to New Orleans. The discovery they made there was profound. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“It’s like, you know, it doesn’t matter what you do, even if you try to replicate an experience down to every last detail, it’ll never be the way it was when it happened naturally the first time.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Andrew and Camryn’s love is like a journey. It’s not always easy, but they make it work. They truly are soul mates. People that were meant to meet, be together and stay together forever. They are passionate, full of love and life. They show that even when things get hard, with the right person by your side, you can get through anything. <br><br><br><br>Andrew and Camryn’s story will forever be unforgettable to me. <i>The Edge of Never </i>is one of my favorite books of all time. Such a beautiful story. J.A. Redmerski is a very talented author, I am a huge fan. The writing was excellent. The book was wonderful, but compared to book one, it just missed the mark a bit for me. It didn’t captivate me like the first book. I still loved it, just not as much. Still a solid 4 stars!<br><i>
  <blockquote>We only have one life. We get one shot at making it worth living. We took our shot and ran like hell with it. And I think we did pretty damn good.</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/5eca6fd0-5dd7-41bf-bc76-5c7529dfbaa6_zps69831e47.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384092341i/6770295.jpg" alt=" photo 5eca6fd0-5dd7-41bf-bc76-5c7529dfbaa6_zps69831e47.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>Our story is over, yes, but our journey isn’t, because we’ll always live on the edge until the day we die.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9813676366738890398"><b>3.5</b><br/><br/>So, it only took like...forever to finally get through this. I love this couple, I really do. And I was hella excited when we were told there'd be a sequel. In fact, I was one of the many that hounded Jessica to write a sequel after I finished TEoN. Because we <i>HAD</i> to have more Andrew and Cam. I fell in love with Andrew, and I loved him in this book. But really...it should've stopped there. The sequel really wasn't needed and I hate that I have to say that. It saddens me. But sometimes the seq</span>
  <span id="freeText9813676366738890398" style="display:none"><b>3.5</b><br /><br />So, it only took like...forever to finally get through this. I love this couple, I really do. And I was hella excited when we were told there'd be a sequel. In fact, I was one of the many that hounded Jessica to write a sequel after I finished TEoN. Because we <i>HAD</i> to have more Andrew and Cam. I fell in love with Andrew, and I loved him in this book. But really...it should've stopped there. The sequel really wasn't needed and I hate that I have to say that. It saddens me. But sometimes the sequels aren't really keeping my excitement anymore. But I still enjoyed it, just not as much as TEON. That one will always be one of my all-time favorites.<br />However, the epilogue was pretty good. Didn't see that coming.<br /><br /><br /><br /><br />EXCERPT<br />Camryn shrieks and I start laughing as we dash away from the cows and toward the car.<br /><br />“Awww, shiiiit!” I yell when I step in a huge pile of it.<br /><br />Camryn cackles with laughter and we both practically stumble the rest of the way through the field, me trying to scrape the shit off the bottom of my shoe while running at the same time and Camryn’s flip-flops getting caught on the ground trying to keep up with her feet.<br /><br />“I can’t believe that just happened!” Camryn laughs as we finally make it back to the car. She arches her body over forward and props her hands on her knees, trying to catch her breath.<br /><br />I’m out of breath, too, but I still relentlessly scrape the bottom of my shoe on the asphalt. “Dammit!” I say, rubbing my foot back and forth.<br /><br />Camryn jumps up on the hood of the car, letting her legs hang over the front. “Can we finally say that we did it?” she asks with laughter in her voice.<br /><br />I stand still finally and catch my breath. I look at her, at how beautiful and bright that smile of hers is and I say, “Yeah, babe, I think we can safely mark it off our list.”<br /><br />“Good!” she says.<br /><br />Then she points behind me. “Do it on the grass,” she says with one side of her mouth pinched into a hard line. “You’re just spreading it around doing it like that.”<br /><br />I hop over into the grass and start rubbing my foot back and forth again. “Since when did you become an expert on shit?”<br /><br />“Better watch your mouth,” she warns, getting into the driver’s seat.<br /><br />“What are you going to do?” I taunt her.<br /><br />She starts the Chevelle and revs the engine a few times pressing on the gas. There’s a cruel gleam in her eyes. She props her left arm across the top of the open window and next thing I know she’s driving slowly past me.<br /><br />I give her the warning eye, but her grin just gets bigger.<br /><br />“I know you won’t leave me here!” I shout as she goes past me.<br /><br />Surely she wouldn’t….<br /><br />She gets farther away and at first I call her bluff and just stand here, watching her get smaller and smaller…<br /><br />Finally, I take off running after the car."<br /><br /><br />Woohooooooooo I love it! Can't wait for November!!!!! It's so far away!!! More Andrew please!!!!! Woohoo!<br /><br /><br />HOLY SHIT!!!! I am just the happiest girl today!!!! This makes me happy happy happppppppppy!!!!!!!!!!!!! SQUEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEE More Andrew Parrish.....yes, yes yes! More Andrew Fucking Parrish! Ahhhhhhhhhh I can't contain my excitement! SO SO SO SO SO SO SO excited!!!!!!!!!!!!!! *deep breaths deep breaths*<br /><br /><br />I may as well give this book FIVE stars right now because I don't think it will be anything less than perfect!!!!!<br /><br />OMFG OMFG!               <span id="reviewTextContainer561878424" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6634557945222502123">Joint review with Kristen/Splage posted at: <a>Swept Away By Romance</a><br/><br/><b>Kristen: 3 ½ Stars<br/>Splage: 3 ½ Stars</b><br/><br/><b><u>What worked</u><br/><br/>Kristen says:</b> One of the things I loved about this book is the amazing characterizations. J. A. Redmerski has a uncanny ability to write characters and dialogue that are so full of life and humanity that they seemingly jump off the pages.<br/>I also loved the road trip. It was fun being on the road with Camryn and Andrew again.<br/><br/><b>Splage says:</b> I am going to start by saying that I chose <i>The Edge </i></span>
  <span id="freeText6634557945222502123" style="display:none">Joint review with Kristen/Splage posted at: <a>Swept Away By Romance</a><br /><br /><b>Kristen: 3 ½ Stars<br />Splage: 3 ½ Stars</b><br /><br /><b><u>What worked</u><br /><br />Kristen says:</b> One of the things I loved about this book is the amazing characterizations. J. A. Redmerski has a uncanny ability to write characters and dialogue that are so full of life and humanity that they seemingly jump off the pages.<br />I also loved the road trip. It was fun being on the road with Camryn and Andrew again.<br /><br /><b>Splage says:</b> I am going to start by saying that I chose <i>The Edge of Never</i> as my number one book of 2012. That being said I was very scared to reopen the perfect and fresh experience I had with it. What I found with <i>The Edge of Always </i>is that it was not a rewrite or a full length epilogue disguised as a book like you often see as a sequel when book 1 has a true and satisfying ending. Camryn and Andrew’s life goes on and it isn’t perfect. They run into to some hard and heartbreaking obstacles. <br /><br /><b><u>What didn’t work</u><br /><br />Kristen says:</b> Unfortunately, the first half of the story didn't fully work for me. It was very <i>slow </i> and I struggled with the initial direction the author took the continuation of Camryn and Andrew's story.<br /><br /><b>Splage says:</b> I enjoyed their continued adventure and rebellious free spirits of Andrew and Camryn, but was it as good as <i>The Edge of Never</i>…no, and unfortunately that is what it is going to be compared to. The writing was flawless, the story telling fabulous, the character depth beautiful, but I didn’t feel there was anything gained by continuing their story. It sort of depressed me until two thirds of the way through the book where I got that happy euphoric feeling again.<br /><br /><b><u>Best scene(s)</u><br /><br />Kristen says:</b> My favorite scene in this book was when Camryn and Andrew revisited New Orleans and came to realize that you can never fully recreate the past. It was such a poignant scene and I loved everything about.<br /><br /><b>Splage says:</b> The Epilogue is a flash forward 15 years and I loved it. I can’t really say too much about it because would give lots away, but after reading it (plus the last third before it) I jumped my rating ½ a point to 3.5 stars.<br /><br /><b><u>Favorite character(s)</u><br /><br />Kristen says:</b> I loved, loved, loved Andrew's character in this story. I adored him in the first book but he really shined in this one.<br /><br /><b>Splage says:</b> Andrew was such a wonderful hero in this story he stayed true to the protective, giving, and sexy character that he was in book 1. <br /><br /><b><u>Overall Thoughts</u><br /><br />Kristen says:</b> While I'm glad I read this story and loved much about it, it didn't capture my imagination or my heart like first one did. I struggle to stay interested and connected during the first half of the book, and even though I loved the characters and the ending, for me, it didn't have the same impact as <i>The Edge of Never</i> (one of my favorite books of 2012). <b>As much as I loved getting more of Camryn and Andrew, and I did, sometimes I feel it's better to leave a good thing alone.</b> ~<b> 3.5 Stars!</b><br /><br /><b>Splage says:</b> Even though <i>The Edge of Always</i> didn’t live up to book 1 (I think that was an impossible task in my eyes), it still was a good read. I wonder to myself if I would have liked it even more if I would have reread <i>The Edge of Never</i> and then gone directly into reading <i>The Edge of Always</i>. It might have given me an overall experience that was unbelievable. ~<b> 3.5 Stars!</b><br /><br /><i>*A copy of the book was provided to Swept Away by Romance by Grand Central Publishing in exchange for an honest review*</i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6634557945222502123" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_536975581" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/536975581" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/536975581?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17374029-the-edge-of-always">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer536975581" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7876633267607300813"><b>EXCERPT AND MORE - > <a href='http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/2013/10/the-edge-of-always-edge-of-never-2-by.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>HERE</a></b><br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/Mzd768v' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382486624i/5915839._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>Edging to a disappointing 3.5 stars</b><br/><br/>This will be a difficult review to write. I loved The <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/495221174' rel='nofollow noopener'>Edge of Never</a>, it was a six star read for me and a top on my list of favorites. <br/><br/><b>I have been waiting F.O.R.E.V.E.R for The Edge of Always and as much as it pains me to say this, I was left disappointed.</b><br/><br/>I need to first put this out there. There are a lot of five star reviews for The Edge of Always and I can understand that. It’s just a matter of taste and personal preference. The s</span>
  <span id="freeText7876633267607300813" style="display:none"><b>EXCERPT AND MORE - &gt; <a href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/2013/10/the-edge-of-always-edge-of-never-2-by.html" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a></b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/Mzd768v" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382486624i/5915839._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Edging to a disappointing 3.5 stars</b><br><br>This will be a difficult review to write. I loved The <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/495221174" rel="nofollow noopener">Edge of Never</a>, it was a six star read for me and a top on my list of favorites. <br><br><b>I have been waiting F.O.R.E.V.E.R for The Edge of Always and as much as it pains me to say this, I was left disappointed.</b><br><br>I need to first put this out there. There are a lot of five star reviews for The Edge of Always and I can understand that. It’s just a matter of taste and personal preference. The sequel did not affect me like the five star reviewers and I guess when it comes down to it, if an author is going to write a sequel on a couple you absolutely love, what can the author write about that will hold your interest?<br><br>I love Andrew and Cam. I love Andrew period and yes one of the reasons is because he has the same name as my husband. So when we leave off from The Edge of Never, it was a HEA right? The two couple is moving forward (this is not a spoiler).<br><br>So, there needs to be tension right for book two? I think this is where I had a hard time in enjoying the book. I couldn’t agree with the tension. I am the type of reader that likes couples to go against the world, where they use their love for each other to work out struggling issues. The issues come from a third party and or external force. I do not like it when the tension is between the Heroine and Hero. It’s because I already went through that. I went through the couple’s struggles in the first book and I simply do not want to go over that again.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/QJLd7Tq" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382486624i/5915840._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So, yes, Cam and Andrew go through issues and as a result of these issues, it creates tension in the relationship. I honestly believe a lot of things could have been resolved with a conversation or just pure logical reasoning. Cam was silly, she frustrated me and I wanted to slap her. If I want to slap anyone in a book, it’s the downfall for me.<br><br>Now, there’s other things that go on and at one point (we all know what I am talking about, if you have read it) I was kind of like, oh yeah this is perking my interest! I want this kind of drama, and then just as I was getting into it, the thing fizzes out.<br><br>And then towards the second half the story drags. I hate to do this because I love Redmerski so much (yes I have a girl crush on her), but I **gasp** skimmed! I know I hide my face in shame. I just didn’t care about this or that, that or this. So what? Big deal? Let’s get something going on.<br><br>I don’t know where the story was suppose to take me. I wanted to feel for Andrew and Cam, but what I got was a young couple going through problems, but reacting kind of ridiculous and then boring.<br><br>I say this though, you may not react the same way as me. If you are true Andrew and Cam fan, please read this book. If there is another book in the series, I will read it. I will read anything by Redmerski because to me, she is one of the top writers. I have faith in her and I just think she may have been snatched by aliens when she wrote this book.<br><br>Sorry, I went there. But I really do love Andrew, Cam and Redmerski. I hope I’m not hated by many after this review.<br><br><i>An ARC was provided in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br>For more, please visit <a href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Jacqueline's Reads</a><br><br><b>Series Order</b><br>The Edge of Never<br><a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00BL3P5E6/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;creativeASIN=B00BL3P5E6&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382487239i/5916147.gif" width="1" height="1" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The Edge of Always<br><a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00BOTU4E8/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;creativeASIN=B00BOTU4E8&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382487239i/5916148.gif" width="1" height="1" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Buddy Read</b> - Tricia :D</span>
  <a data-text-id="7876633267607300813" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/536280311" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/536280311?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781455549016" href="/book/show/17557577-the-edge-of-always">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer536280311" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16229511713096687865"><b>
  <u>My Thoughts:</u>
</b><br/><br/>♫ It was great being back with one of my favorite couples, Andrew and Camryn, and even though I didn't think it was as good as the first book, it was still very enjoyable.<br/><br/>♫ Of course, what I thought might happen, happened and it certainly lead to some drama but I liked how Andrew and eventually Camryn handled things. <br/><br/>♫ I loved, loved, loved the road trip! I think that's one of my favorite things! <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384147369i/6792577.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>♫ But what in the heck happened in Florida? That was sooo crazy and seemed a little </span>
  <span id="freeText16229511713096687865" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>My Thoughts:</u>
</b><br><br>♫ It was great being back with one of my favorite couples, Andrew and Camryn, and even though I didn't think it was as good as the first book, it was still very enjoyable.<br><br>♫ Of course, what I thought might happen, happened and it certainly lead to some drama but I liked how Andrew and eventually Camryn handled things. <br><br>♫ I loved, loved, loved the road trip! I think that's one of my favorite things! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384147369i/6792577.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>♫ But what in the heck happened in Florida? That was sooo crazy and seemed a little pointless? I didn't realize until I saw the excerpt for <i>Song of the Fireflies</i>, that it was possibly to introduce Bray and Elias?<br><br>♫ Andrew is just sooo sweet and he just gets Camryn. I love how they are with each other. I still love their tattoos, their singing together and I especially loved all their little "promises" they were making and got a kick out of how it was "incorporated" later on!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/502667.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>♫ I wasn't too happy with how tricky JAR was especially that part at about the 73% point. I had a feeling it would go the way I was thinking but it did make me second guess things. <br><br>♫ Okay, sooo, I didn't really like the Epilogue. I didn't like who's POV it was from either. It felt so disconnected and I didn't believe that Andrew and Camryn would stay away that long. Also, even though I was happy with how things wrapped up, she <i>really</i> wrapped them up. I'm not sure how I feel about fifteen years going by. <br><br>♫ Also, technically the book stops at 85%. I hate that because I had no clue there were excerpts and info for other books tacked on. I wish somehow they could make the percentage for just the story and anything else would be over 100% especially because it made me think something crazy was going to happen!<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384160913ra/6798313.gif" width="400" height="070" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>❤ “I did it in the shower just minutes ago. You should’ve been there.”<br><br>❤ “Remember when I said you were the world to me? You asked me to remind you if you ever forgot. Well, I’m reminding you now.”<br></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=the-bad-boy-look">the-bad-boy-look</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=cat-heart-these-books">cat-heart-these-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer571430820" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14974110651984066127"> <b>4 Breathtaking stars!!</b>	<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383867943i/6691787.jpg' width='450' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>After a very bumpy path, Andrew and Camryn are finally together, with a baby on the way and completely happy. <br/>They have all their lives ahead of them to make new plans and get to know the world. <br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380436893ra/883339.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>But plans can change anytime and when tragedy knocks at their door, they must deal with the most difficult path they probably had to walk through.<br/>And find out the place they want to belong in the world… when the world doesn’t seem like a good place to be anymore. <br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383867943i/6691788.jpg' width='300' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I really liked</span>
  <span id="freeText14974110651984066127" style="display:none"> <b>4 Breathtaking stars!!</b>	<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383867943i/6691787.jpg" width="450" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After a very bumpy path, Andrew and Camryn are finally together, with a baby on the way and completely happy. <br>They have all their lives ahead of them to make new plans and get to know the world. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380436893ra/883339.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But plans can change anytime and when tragedy knocks at their door, they must deal with the most difficult path they probably had to walk through.<br>And find out the place they want to belong in the world… when the world doesn’t seem like a good place to be anymore. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383867943i/6691788.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really liked this book. I did. <br>I know I’ll eventually get back to it a re-read some of my favorite parts. But I didn’t liked it, by far, as I did the first one. <br>The best thing about this book is that we had so much more of Andrew’s mind… and that’s a great place to be. *wink* <br>I couldn’t feel as connected as I felt in the first one, nor I have the absolutely necessity to: <i>keep reading ‘til it ends or my eyes close with sleep. Whichever comes first.</i> I’m sure you know that feeling.<br>But do I think that you should read it? YES. Especially if you read the first and loved it. <br>(And if you haven’t read the first… why are you reading this? And WHY AREN’T YOU READING IT??!)<br>It was not a bad book, far from it, it was pretty damn good… just not as much as the first. But that’s understandable… it’s a hard level to achieve. <br>Go read this now, Andrew Parrish is a book-boyfriend you really can’t miss! </span>
  <a data-text-id="14974110651984066127" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_536194484" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/536194484" />
    <a title="M. ~ B&amp;B" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14479657-m-b-b"><img alt="M. ~ B&amp;B" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435261660p2/14479657.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/536194484?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="M. ~ B&amp;B" class="user" itemprop="url" name="M. ~ B&amp;B" href="/user/show/14479657-m-b-b">M. ~ B&amp;B</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17374029-the-edge-of-always">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14479657-m-b-b?shelf=yes-i-cried">yes-i-cried</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14479657-m-b-b?shelf=thought-provoking">thought-provoking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14479657-m-b-b?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14479657-m-b-b?shelf=inspiring-and-beautiful">inspiring-and-beautiful</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14479657-m-b-b?shelf=relationship-drama-kept-to-minimum">relationship-drama-kept-to-minimum</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer536194484" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15864732438050397201">***Warning: This review contains huge spoilers for <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081272.The_Edge_of_Never__The_Edge_of_Never___1_' title='The Edge of Never (The Edge of Never, #1) by J.A. Redmerski' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Edge of Never</a>***<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>In five months I found myself with him, fell in total, unconitional crazy love, truly learned how to live, met pactically his entire family and quickly felt like a prt of them, went through a life- and- death journey with Andrew, got pregnant and engaged. All in five months' time. And now here we are facing another hardship. And he's still with me every step of the way.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>And Andrew is back!! Give me a moment here.. </span>
  <span id="freeText15864732438050397201" style="display:none">***Warning: This review contains huge spoilers for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081272.The_Edge_of_Never__The_Edge_of_Never___1_" title="The Edge of Never (The Edge of Never, #1) by J.A. Redmerski" rel="nofollow noopener">The Edge of Never</a>***<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>In five months I found myself with him, fell in total, unconitional crazy love, truly learned how to live, met pactically his entire family and quickly felt like a prt of them, went through a life- and- death journey with Andrew, got pregnant and engaged. All in five months' time. And now here we are facing another hardship. And he's still with me every step of the way.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>And Andrew is back!! Give me a moment here.. ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥<br><br>Okay, where was I? Right. The review. You all should know I can and will never get enough of Andrew Parrish, so if Ms. Redmerski decided to write 10 more books about him, even if it was a boring HEA, I would read them all and rate them all 5 stars, because I love him so damn much. So as Camryn would say, I may be a bit biased here. <br><br><i>The Edge of Always</i> picks up right where the first book left off.<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>A few months ago, when I was laid up in that hospital bed, I didn't think I'd be alive today much less be expecting a baby and engaged to an angel with a dirty mouth.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Andrew is still as hilarious as ever. He may be even more wonderful in the sequel. I laughed so much in the beginning and I fell in love with him all over again. Camryn and Andrew have grown up a lot. They're wise and mature for their age, but at the same time they're still that playful boy and girl who met on the bus and who keep teasing each other and making each other laugh. <br><br>I think the synopsis covers the story pretty well. It's not all good times and every couple goes through hardships at one point in their relationship. Unfortunately for Andrew and Camryn, they can't catch a break and after going through what they went through with Andrew, another tragedy strikes them.<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Now, there comes a time in a person's life when you have to face something so horrible that you feel like you'll never be the same person again. It's like something dark swoops down from somewhere above and steals every shred of happiness you have ever fet and all you can do is watch it, feel it go, knowing that no matter what you do in your life that you'll never be able to get it back. Everybody goes through this at least once. No one is immune.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>We all deal with problems in a different way and Camryn deals with problems by trying to forget or ignoring they exist. Much like she did in the first book. Luckily she still has Andrew who moves heaven and earth and uses his brilliant mind and wisdom to help Camryn get through whatever she's going through and make her feel like smiling again.<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>You're like a philosopher with tattoos.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Andrew and Camryn learn to live in the moment again together, enjoy the little things, do whatever they enjoy and whenever they enjoy it. They have moments of weakness, strength, stupidity and happiness. This book is about not letting your fears stop you from doing what you want the most. Not conforming to society's wishes, but doing what makes <i>you</i> happy. And knowing that everything happens for a reason.<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I'm not saying that people who choose to stay in one place all their life and raise a family are wrong. It's the people who don't want to live like that, who dream about being something more, doing something more, but never pull it off because they let fear stop them before they get started.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>I am so sad that Andrew and Camryn's story is over now. I cried during the last few chapters and I can't even tell you why. I think it's partly because I love them so much and another part of it is that there's a lot that I feel I can relate to. Their story kind of made me wonder if I made the right choices in my own life.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>We only have one life. We get one shot at making it worth living. We took our shot and ran like hell with it.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>***<br><br>My song for Andrew and Camryn is Between the Raindrops by Lifehouse ft. Natasha Bedingfield. I think it fits perfectly. I played it on repeat while reading and the song alone made me cry. I'll leave you with the lyrics and if you haven't heard this song yet, go YouTube it.<br><blockquote>
  <i>Look around<br>There's no one but you and me<br>Right here and now<br>The way it was meant to be<br>There's a smile on my face<br>Knowing that together everything that's in our way<br>We're better than alright<br><br>Walking between the raindrops<br>Riding the aftershock beside you<br>Off into the sunset<br>Living like there's nothing left to lose<br>Chasing after gold mines<br>Crossing the fine lines we knew<br>Hold on and take a breath<br>I'll be here every step<br>Walking between the raindrops with you<br><br>Take me now<br>The world's such a crazy place<br>When the walls come down<br>You'll know I'm here to stay<br>There's nothing I would change<br>Knowing that together everything that's in our way<br>We're better than alright<br><br>Walking between the raindrops<br>Riding the aftershock beside you<br>Off into the sunset<br>Living like there's nothing left to lose<br>Chasing after gold mines<br>Crossing the fine lines we knew<br>Hold on and take a breath<br>I'll be here every step<br>Walking between the raindrops with you</i>
</blockquote>Lifehouse ft. Natasha Bedingfield - Between the Raindrops<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379787774i/499994._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I just wanna sit here and stare at this cover all day.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="15864732438050397201" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty"><img alt="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1481371426p2/13273769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/536257712?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty">Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17374029-the-edge-of-always">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer536257712" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3237239987463249108"><br/> <br/><b>
  <i>“Our story is over, yes, but our journey isn't, because we'll always live on the edge until the day we die.” </i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383947489i/6714290._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Andrew Parrish... Need I say more?!<br/>I love this guy! <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383947489i/6714291.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Cam-<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383947489i/6714292._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Andrew has always amazed me. He amazed me with the way his mind worked. The way he could look at me without saying anything and make me feel like the most important person in the world. He amazed me with how he could always be so positive even when life was falling apart around him. And how he could make a light shine in the</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText3237239987463249108" style="display:none"><br> <br><b>
  <i>“Our story is over, yes, but our journey isn't, because we'll always live on the edge until the day we die.” </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383947489i/6714290._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Andrew Parrish... Need I say more?!<br>I love this guy! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383947489i/6714291.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cam-<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383947489i/6714292._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Andrew has always amazed me. He amazed me with the way his mind worked. The way he could look at me without saying anything and make me feel like the most important person in the world. He amazed me with how he could always be so positive even when life was falling apart around him. And how he could make a light shine in the darkest recesses of my mind when I thought that I’d never see another light there again."</i>
</b><br><br>Okay on to the story... :)<br>Since we read <u>The Edge Of Never</u> we all loved Andrew and Cam's story...<br>Now as the story continues after Andrews Tumor and Cam and Andrew back to reality 5 months later...<br><br><b>
  <i>"Today is the first day of the rest of our lives."</i>
</b><br><br>With a baby on the way the road and traveling isn't an option.<br>When something so sad and unfortunate happens Cam, looses herself and Andrew being themost awesome Fiancé in history decides that they need to do what they love... Travel...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383947489i/6714293.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Life on the road... <br>The journey...<br>The fun...<br>The experience...<br><br><b>
  <i>“Because this is our life. We met on the road; we grew to know and to love each other on the road. It's where we were meant to be for however long, and it's what we're going to do until it becomes clear that we're meant to do something else.” </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383947489i/6714294._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Cam and Andrew on the road again with special moments, lots of love, passionand great laughs<br>They find themselves back in New Orleans- a sense of dejavu overcomes them. <br>Only now they realize that life isn't about reliving old memories, its about creating new ones.. <br><br><b>
  <i>“You’re the world to me,” I whisper onto<br>her lips. “I hope you never forget that.”<br>“I’ll never forget,” she whispers back.. “But if I ever do, for<br>whatever reason, I hope you’ll always find a way to remind me.”<br>...“Always.” </i>
</b><br><br>Yes there are good days, bad days, crazy days and some mad experiences.<br><br><b>
  <i>It’s like, you know, it doesn’t matter what you do, even if you try to replicate an experience down to every last detail, it’ll never be the way it was when it happened naturally the first time.” </i>
</b><br><br>From the first moment Cam and Andrew met, we knew these two were in it for the long haul. Soul mates. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I promise to love you forever in this life and wherever we go in the afterlife, because I know I can't go on in any life unless you're in it too.” </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383947489i/6714295.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>J.A Redmerski is so good with words, seriously this woman touches your heart with her writing. <br><br>Life doesn't end when you meet someone, and after marriage most loose that spark.<br>Not everyone wants a white picket fence. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383947489i/6714296._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>These two keep the fun in life, the journey to the destination being unknown, living life to the fullest.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Our story is over, yes, but our journey isn’t, because we’ll always live on the edge until the day we die."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383947489i/6714297.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For anyone who hasn't read series, you are missing out because I wish I could go back to the start.</span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17374029-the-edge-of-always">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer639991128" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5596513782443386553"><b>3.5 'Growing up' Stars </b><br/><br/><i>Can their Love survive anything????</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384205501i/6813462.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>"...here we are facing another hardship."</b><i>Yes, there's more devastating drama..... </i><br/><br/>Camryn needs to come to terms with EVERYTHING, including her greatest fear.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384205502i/6813463._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>'The Edge of Always,' is about a deep, deep love.... Unbreakable, apart from one thing... And it's that which scares Camryn. Her worries are magnified because of everything that's happened to her in her troubled life.<br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384205502i/6813464._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>"...it was fate that we met on that bus in Kansas..."</b><br/><br/><br/>It was, dare I </span>
  <span id="freeText5596513782443386553" style="display:none"><b>3.5 'Growing up' Stars </b><br><br><i>Can their Love survive anything????</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384205501i/6813462.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"...here we are facing another hardship."</b><i>Yes, there's more devastating drama..... </i><br><br>Camryn needs to come to terms with EVERYTHING, including her greatest fear.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384205502i/6813463._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>'The Edge of Always,' is about a deep, deep love.... Unbreakable, apart from one thing... And it's that which scares Camryn. Her worries are magnified because of everything that's happened to her in her troubled life.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384205502i/6813464._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>"...it was fate that we met on that bus in Kansas..."</b><br><br><br>It was, dare I say, a little slow in places but then in some places I would love or swoon or smile or cry. I think a slow detailed burn is the authors writing style. I like how her books make me feel by the end.. I can accept her details (as long as I read fast!!!) much like I accept an old friend.... Andrew was the driving force for me, him and his beautiful relationship with Camryn....<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384205869i/6813572._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I love the sentiment behind the book, it's life affirming; makes you think about living in the moment, facing your fears and making everything count. J.A. Redmerski took me on a journey and, for me, it came full circle and left me with that satisfied book feeling.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384206219i/6813811._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>♥ Br with Aimie, Barb, Deanna &amp; Shannon xoxo</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8448197650415957011">3.5 Stars <br/><br/>I couldn't get enough of "The Edge Of Never" so had to read this one. Did I love it as much? No, it fell a bit short of my expectations, but "The Edge Of Never" was a very hard act to follow. Still this was a decent read, was about romance, my favorite genre, and kept me turning the pages ;)</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/537466033" />
    <a title="Asser" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5322260-asser"><img alt="Asser" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586302845p2/5322260.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/537466033?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Asser" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Asser" href="/user/show/5322260-asser">Asser</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17374029-the-edge-of-always">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5322260-asser?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5322260-asser?shelf=that-cover">that-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5322260-asser?shelf=highly-anticipated-books-of-2013">highly-anticipated-books-of-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5322260-asser?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5322260-asser?shelf=road-trips">road-trips</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5322260-asser?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5322260-asser?shelf=i-own-a-copy">i-own-a-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5322260-asser?shelf=alternating-pov">alternating-pov</a>
