        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer537466033" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5935675393668650574"><i>
  <b>"You're the world to me," I whisper onto her lips. "I hope you never forget that."<br/><br/>"I'll never forget that... But if I ever do, for whatever reason, I hope you'll always find a way to remind me."<br/><br/>"Always..."</b>
</i><br/><br/><b>5-STAR WORTHY!!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435115ra/879005.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Beautiful love story. Simply amazing.</b><br/><br/>I don't think this book could have been written any better.<br/><br/>Andrew and Camryn's another spontaneous expedition... <i>The Edge of Always</i> exceeded my expectations. Once again, J.A. Redmerski made me fall in love with the characters that I fell </span>
  <span id="freeText5935675393668650574" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"You're the world to me," I whisper onto her lips. "I hope you never forget that."<br><br>"I'll never forget that... But if I ever do, for whatever reason, I hope you'll always find a way to remind me."<br><br>"Always..."</b>
</i><br><br><b>5-STAR WORTHY!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435115ra/879005.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Beautiful love story. Simply amazing.</b><br><br>I don't think this book could have been written any better.<br><br>Andrew and Camryn's another spontaneous expedition... <i>The Edge of Always</i> exceeded my expectations. Once again, J.A. Redmerski made me fall in love with the characters that I fell in love with a year ago.<br><br><i>The Edge of Always</i> narrates another journey of Andrew and Camryn's life. It was told mostly from Andrew's point of view and began four months after the ending of <i>The Edge of Never</i>. Andrew and Camryn were engaged and expecting a baby. But then tragedy struck which brought them to take another road trip.<br><br><b>
  <i>Learn to take risks. If you won't, the answer will always be a no.</i>
</b><br><br>Why I love the story of Andrew and Camryn the most is because it never fails to captivate me. Like in <i>The Edge of Never</i>, I was drawn to it from the very beginning. I was truly invested with the characters and I never got bored I actually finished it in one day. This novel was so good I was so overwhelmed throughout my entire read. I wanted to cry happy tears when I finished it because the ending couldn't have been more perfect.<br><br>I don't think there will be any fictional characters in the future that I will love as much as I love Andrew and Camryn. I really enjoyed reading this and although I'm sad because it finally came to an end, I am also happy because my favorite characters got their perfect happily-ever-after.<br><br><i>
  <b>"Our story is over, yes, but our journey isn't, because we'll always live on the edge until the day we die."</b>
</i><br><br>I definitely know for sure that I will never ever forget Andrew and Camryn's story and this series will always have a piece of my heart. If you are a huge fan like me, you will love <i>The Edge of Always</i> as much as I did.<br><br><b>LOVED IT.</b><br><br>------------------------------------------------------------------------<br><br><b>BEFORE READING:</b><br><br><u>
  <b>
    <i>Update!!</i>
  </b>
</u><br><b>The COVER!!!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1363188907l/17374029.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>OH MY GOD!</b> I can't <b>breathe</b>! LOOK at that cover! <i>
  <b>He is so freakin' HOT!</b>

<div id="review_1229205527" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1229205527" />
    <a title="Vina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18492568-vina"><img alt="Vina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587590331p2/18492568.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1229205527?book_show_action=true">Mar 16, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vina" href="/user/show/18492568-vina">Vina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18492568-vina?shelf=normal">normal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1229205527" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15771325491059772861">I liked this book for a few reasons. I despised it for even more .<br/><br/><b>“I guess sometimes the greatest memories are made in the most unlikely of places, further proof that spontaneity is more rewarding than a meticulously planned life.”</b><br/>I still love Andrew but this book really didn't do for me what the first one did. I felt like there were alot of ideas and stories that got started in this book but then just got dropped. These seemed to be there for no reason and that kind of thing really turns me off</span>
  <span id="freeText15771325491059772861" style="display:none">I liked this book for a few reasons. I despised it for even more .<br><br><b>“I guess sometimes the greatest memories are made in the most unlikely of places, further proof that spontaneity is more rewarding than a meticulously planned life.”</b><br>I still love Andrew but this book really didn't do for me what the first one did. I felt like there were alot of ideas and stories that got started in this book but then just got dropped. These seemed to be there for no reason and that kind of thing really turns me off in a story. I felt that in book 1 we really watched their relationship evolve and the emotions were deep and real. In this book I felt that they were just reliving what happened in book one. I also felt a disconnect between Andrew and Camryn. I felt it from her side, something in her changed and she was pretty much afraid to love him this time around. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420442127ra/13226322.gif" width="400" height="225" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The scene where Andrew found out Camryn had been taking the pain pills had to be one of them most infuriating for me. He's clearly upset and angry, but remains quiet and then completely understands and forgives her. I realize they are just characters in a book, but they lose some of their humanity when they don't show proper emotions and are made into the "perfect man, woman, fiancé, spouse, etc.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>This book, for the most part, had me wondering where the hell did Camryn from the first book go?I felt like I was reading about a totally different character. She seemed completely self absorbed only invested in her own feelings and never once asking Andrew his.The book was so focused on Camryn's reaction to it that it seemed like Andrew was almost forgotten. After all, it was something that impacted them both and I would like to have seen more how he handled it as well.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422881526i/13558075.jpg" width="500" height="264" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Though it doesn't consist of the most realistic circumstances,I really loved it when they got on the road again. This series is about letting go, living freely, taking chances and having no regrets! I'd be lying if I said it didn't inspire me to loosen up and live a little more without worrying so much.<br><br>Overall it was an OK read. I did not hate it but I did not love it as much as the first book.<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="15771325491059772861" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_536225499" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/536225499" />
    <a title="Ang (Sizzling Pages)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13629682-ang-sizzling-pages"><img alt="Ang (Sizzling Pages)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1541857150p2/13629682.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/536225499?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ang (Sizzling Pages)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ang (Sizzling Pages)" href="/user/show/13629682-ang-sizzling-pages">Ang (Sizzling Pages)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17374029-the-edge-of-always">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer536225499" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10323955180621879249"><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://angelas-sizzling-pages.blogspot.com'>http://angelas-sizzling-pages.blogspo...</a><br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.sizzlingpages.com'>http://www.sizzlingpages.com</a><br/>4 out of 5 drama filled stars<br/><br/>Truth be told, I was a little apprehensive about reading "THE EDGE OF ALWAYS”. "THE EDGE OF NEVER" was such a profound, emotionally driven tale, I wasn’t sure if continuing Andrew and Camryn’s story would hold the same level of excellence. In the end, I am delighted to see the road these two have travelled. <br/><br/>The story flowed quite nicely, alternating from each of their POV’s, but was a bit slow paced.</span>
  <span id="freeText10323955180621879249" style="display:none"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://angelas-sizzling-pages.blogspot.com">http://angelas-sizzling-pages.blogspo...</a><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.sizzlingpages.com">http://www.sizzlingpages.com</a><br>4 out of 5 drama filled stars<br><br>Truth be told, I was a little apprehensive about reading "THE EDGE OF ALWAYS”. "THE EDGE OF NEVER" was such a profound, emotionally driven tale, I wasn’t sure if continuing Andrew and Camryn’s story would hold the same level of excellence. In the end, I am delighted to see the road these two have travelled. <br><br>The story flowed quite nicely, alternating from each of their POV’s, but was a bit slow paced. It started off sweet, portraying their lives after Andrew’s recovery, somewhat settling down, and on the road to bliss. But, as fate plays a hand, heartbreak falls onto their path. Cam becomes devastated, leaving Andrew determined to heal her the only way he knows how…. Road trip!<br> <br>Their journey to healing Cam and Andrew dealing with his own demons was a lovely story, but it did not hold the angst element as the first installment. However, I liked the way Cam’s character grew, the way she matured, learned from her mistakes, sought closure and dealt with her misfortunes. I loved the strength of Andrew’s persona. Dealing with his own hardships, Andrew looked deep within his soul to find the courage needed to be Cam’s rock. As always, it is Andrew’s love and fearlessness that heals Camryn’s broken spirit. These two compliment each other, and they are a perfect couple in every way. And most importantly...Andrew is HAWT!<br><br>In conclusion, this is a story about unconditional love, finding inner strength, self-discovery, facing fears, and learning to command one’s destiny. Like Orpheus and Eurydice, Andrew and Cam’s story is a “tragic tale of true love”. They are “two lost souls swimming in a fish bowl” that are destined to be together. They are indestructible. <br><br>I highly recommend “Edge of Always" and it was a good read, even though I would have preferred the story to hold a tad more excitement and intensity. I was really happy to see their HEA and a possibility of a spin-off series.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383705642i/6639367._SX540_.jpg" width='“100"' height='“100"' alt="description”/&gt;&lt;br /&gt;" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="10323955180621879249" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_747594377" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/747594377" />
    <a title="Carol (StarAngel&#39;s Reviews) Allen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6294320-carol-starangel-s-reviews-allen"><img alt="Carol (StarAngel&#39;s Reviews) Allen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1386893634p2/6294320.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/747594377?book_show_action=true">Oct 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carol (StarAngel&#39;s Reviews) Allen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carol (StarAngel&#39;s Reviews) Allen" href="/user/show/6294320-carol-starangel-s-reviews-allen">Carol (StarAngel&#39;s Reviews) Allen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17374029-the-edge-of-always">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6294320-carol-starangel-s-reviews-allen?shelf=arc-reviewed">arc-reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6294320-carol-starangel-s-reviews-allen?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6294320-carol-starangel-s-reviews-allen?shelf=emotional-roller-coaster">emotional-roller-coaster</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6294320-carol-starangel-s-reviews-allen?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer747594377" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1341598558464195799"><strong>**** 3 ½ Fast Paced Stars ****</strong> <br/><br/><em>ARC provided by Grand Central Publishing via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.</em><br/><br/>I’m a bit confused on how to word this review since I am currently sitting on fence questioning whether to tilt to the left (liked) or tilt to the right (disliked). I was so excited to be chosen to read an ARC of this book since I fell in love with Camryn and Andrew in “The Edge of Never”.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383088123i/6383351.jpg' alt='' width='275' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I think what has me leaning to the right is that the book skips so fast from days to weeks </span>
  <span id="freeText1341598558464195799" style="display:none"><strong>**** 3 ½ Fast Paced Stars ****</strong> <br><br><em>ARC provided by Grand Central Publishing via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.</em><br><br>I’m a bit confused on how to word this review since I am currently sitting on fence questioning whether to tilt to the left (liked) or tilt to the right (disliked). I was so excited to be chosen to read an ARC of this book since I fell in love with Camryn and Andrew in “The Edge of Never”.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383088123i/6383351.jpg" alt="" width="275" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think what has me leaning to the right is that the book skips so fast from days to weeks to months and then a mess of years. Plus there really isn’t any angst in the story and if there is…we only have to wait a couple of pages till breathing a sigh of relief. I didn’t cry like I did with the first book, I didn’t connect with the characters in this book but…….I did like the overall premise of the story.<br><br>The book starts with Camryn and Andrew living together in Texas and Andrew is recovered from his brain tumor. Because of certain tragic events that happen and that happened in the past, Camryn starts to recoil into her mind. This prompts her to try anything in order not to feel anymore. Andrew can feel the tension between her and the rest of her friends and family and decides enough is enough and he takes matters into his own hands.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383088123i/6383352.jpg" alt="" width="183" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This prompts another road trip for as long as it takes Camryn to want to live life to the fullest again. They have their ups and downs on this journey both psychically and mentally while they experience the wonderful love they shared through the first book.<br><br>I was happy to have read this book and have the story of Camryn and Andrew completed. My recommendation is, if you read the 1st book, try this one…every one has their own taste in books and yours may be completely different from mine!<br><br>Cheers!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1341598558464195799" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer559924903" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer12717423700470921692"><b>3 stars??</b><br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=nck39u' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388503843ra/7854973.gif' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=fabx1w' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388503843ra/7854974.gif' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=2ic8bvm' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388503843ra/7854975.gif' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Uh...<br/><br/>This wasn't bad. Not really. But dare I say that this book is unnecessary? I mean, I finished <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081272.The_Edge_of_Never__The_Edge_of_Never___1_' title='The Edge of Never (The Edge of Never, #1) by J.A. Redmerski' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Edge of Never</a> (which I LOVED), totally satisfied with the ending. Andrew's surgery was successful and they were happy. HEA. Yay!<br/><br/>I was satisfied with it. Totally. No complaints. <br/><br/>And then we have this book, and I'm sorry to say, I was underwhelmed. After the reading the epicness that was The Edge of Never, its follow up trudged and meandered along until it was over.<br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=2rffvar' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388504003ra/7854995.gif' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>To be </span>
  <span id="freeText12717423700470921692" style="display:none"><b>3 stars??</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=nck39u" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388503843ra/7854973.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=fabx1w" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388503843ra/7854974.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2ic8bvm" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388503843ra/7854975.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Uh...<br><br>This wasn't bad. Not really. But dare I say that this book is unnecessary? I mean, I finished <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081272.The_Edge_of_Never__The_Edge_of_Never___1_" title="The Edge of Never (The Edge of Never, #1) by J.A. Redmerski" rel="nofollow noopener">The Edge of Never</a> (which I LOVED), totally satisfied with the ending. Andrew's surgery was successful and they were happy. HEA. Yay!<br><br>I was satisfied with it. Totally. No complaints. <br><br>And then we have this book, and I'm sorry to say, I was underwhelmed. After the reading the epicness that was The Edge of Never, its follow up trudged and meandered along until it was over.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2rffvar" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388504003ra/7854995.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>To be fair, some things did happen but honestly, I don't think I need to read through 464 pages to know that those things happened. A novella would have sufficed. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/ES9Oaf0" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434499ra/876990.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I still love Andrew Parrish though, and Camryn was okay. The stuff that she and Andrew went through in this book was tragic and sad. I get that, but 464 pages? <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=35kj4hd" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388504863ra/7855299.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Other than what Camryn went through and Andrew's <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[health scare <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, not much happened in this book. The writing was very good but again, the book was just too long.<br><br>*sigh*<br><br>Still, if you love Andrew and Camryn enough and The Edge of Never is one of your favorite book of all time, give this book a try. <br><br><i>ARC provided GCP Forever in exchange for an honest review.</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer525693518126340071">I was really, really looking forward to this book. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081272.The_Edge_of_Never__The_Edge_of_Never___1_' title='The Edge of Never (The Edge of Never, #1) by J.A. Redmerski' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Edge of Never</a> was one of my favorites of 2013 and it will remain so. However, when I recommend it, I will recommend it as a standalone. I'm not going to get into what didn't work. At first I thought it was the weird feel the story took in the beginning but in the end it felt weird all together. I really feel like I should give it 2 stars but there were glimpses of the same characters I so fell in love with in the first book I decided to bump</span>
  <span id="freeText525693518126340071" style="display:none">I was really, really looking forward to this book. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081272.The_Edge_of_Never__The_Edge_of_Never___1_" title="The Edge of Never (The Edge of Never, #1) by J.A. Redmerski" rel="nofollow noopener">The Edge of Never</a> was one of my favorites of 2013 and it will remain so. However, when I recommend it, I will recommend it as a standalone. I'm not going to get into what didn't work. At first I thought it was the weird feel the story took in the beginning but in the end it felt weird all together. I really feel like I should give it 2 stars but there were glimpses of the same characters I so fell in love with in the first book I decided to bump up my rating. Overall it was a big disappointment for me. Oh, I forgot to metion, I started this book the day it came out and this was me...<br><br><a href="http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/smr_zps296e3df9.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I thought maybe it was just me so I took a <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381345527ra/4735584.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Because I wanted to love this book so much I thought maybe I just wasn't feeling it and I need to revisit it another time. However, each time I came back it was more<br><br><a href="http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/tumblr_mdpsqptQ1b1r8vq22_zps12912dbf.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I had a goal to finish it before the year was out just to get it off my currently reading shelf. I finished it at 11:50 pm New Years Eve. I'm glad it's over, I wouldn't recommend it though. Like I said there glimpses of the same magic from book one but it wasn't even close to being enough to make this one good. <br><br></span>

<div id="review_536545620" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/536545620" />
    <a title="Maria " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5769334-maria"><img alt="Maria " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600318539p2/5769334.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/536545620?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maria " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maria " href="/user/show/5769334-maria">Maria </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17374029-the-edge-of-always">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer536545620" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5966991909882689159"><b>5 EXTREMELY SWEET AND INSANELY SEXY HEARTS!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383878837i/6694306.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383878837i/6694306.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383878837i/6694306.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383878837i/6694306.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383878837i/6694306.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"You think we're lost?"<br/><br/>I tilt my head back a little and look up at the stars behind her and say, "In society, maybe. But together, no. I think we're right where we need to be."</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>REACTION AFTER READING THE BOOK</b><br/><br/>My heart<br/>Is just full of happiness right now!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384052425ra/6757081.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384052425ra/6757082.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384052425ra/6757083.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>To date, The Edge of Never and now The Edge of Always easily became my favorite book of all time.<br/><br/>Before I start and share my passionate love for this book. I'll start with a short <b>GIST</b><br/><br/><i>Just when things a</i></span>
  <span id="freeText5966991909882689159" style="display:none"><b>5 EXTREMELY SWEET AND INSANELY SEXY HEARTS!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383878837i/6694306.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383878837i/6694306.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383878837i/6694306.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383878837i/6694306.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383878837i/6694306.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"You think we're lost?"<br><br>I tilt my head back a little and look up at the stars behind her and say, "In society, maybe. But together, no. I think we're right where we need to be."</i>
</b><br><br><b>REACTION AFTER READING THE BOOK</b><br><br>My heart<br>Is just full of happiness right now!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384052425ra/6757081.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384052425ra/6757082.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384052425ra/6757083.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To date, The Edge of Never and now The Edge of Always easily became my favorite book of all time.<br><br>Before I start and share my passionate love for this book. I'll start with a short <b>GIST</b><br><br><i>Just when things are starting to fall into place... unexpected things happen that could possibly tear them apart.</i><br><br>Camryn and Andrew met on a Greyhound bus in Kansas.<br>They met. Got to know each other. Went on a roadtrip. Helped each other. Fell in love.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384052425i/6757084.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They both didn't have any idea how that would change their life forever.<br><br>A few months after their roadtrip together, Camryn and Andrew couldn't be more happier.<br>Things was starting to fall together.<br>They made plans for their future.<br>They made arrangements.<br>They had to as they were expecting a baby girl along the way.<br>But something happened.<br>Something unexpected that pushed Camryn over the edge.<br>She tries to hide it like she did a thousand times before but this time Andrew was there.<br>He was there to make sure Camryn doesn't go through her struggles alone.<br>He wasn't going to let her go.<br>He wasn't going to let her fall apart without him.<br>He was going to be there for her no matter what happens.<br>Even if it kills him.<br><br><b>OVERALL THOUGHTS</b><br><br>I just thought this book was really beautiful.<br>Both of them are. <br>I loved the first one, but this book really sealed the deal for me. This is my favorite books of all time. <br>It touched me in ways other books couldn't. <br><br>It was a slow start I agree but I feel like it wouldn't be as heartfelt if the book was too rushed or something. It felt beautiful. It felt real. <br><br>I liked how Camryn and Andrew's relationship turned out. I knew there were loose ends on the last book with Camryn and I loved how Andrew helped her get over that. It was just beautiful and heartwarming and endearing and... Well I couldn't think of any more adjectives as of the moment that would describe how wonderful this book really made me feel. It took me up and down and all around! It was a complete rollercoaster ride.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384052425i/6757085.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think the highlight of this story is really just about love. How love can heal everything. How love could mend broken things. I loved how Andrew showed Camryn how much he loves her no matter what. He never, not once, ever made her forget how much she means to him. He was just perfect. Andrew just couldn't stop swooning me until I am absolutely crazy for him. He was just perfect. I really wish I could find a guy like him. <br><br>Camryn. Although I didn't really agree on some of the decisions she made on this book and on the past one, I still liked her. People cope with pain and loss at different levels and I guess she just had too much and she just broke. Luckily, Andrew was there to pick up all the pieces and mend it back together.<br><br>I cried. Again. Seriously. For the nth time I really cried for this book. I am both happy and sad that its finally come to a close. I enjoyed the giggles that I get when Andrew made his moves on Camryn. I cried when it seems that the problems were pushing them away from each other. I got excited when they were going to go back on a roadtrip. I was happy and again teary-eyed when they finally got their happily ever after. <br><br>Love is such a special thing isn't it? I love J.A Redmerski so much I think I'll kiss her a million times when I see her.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384052425ra/6757086.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When Camryn and Andrew did their little gigs every now and then, I absolutely imagined Andrew singing the song "Your Song" to Camryn. Of course, its the Cameron Mitchell version is what I was talking about. I attached a short snippet of the lyrics below.<br><br><b>
  <i>It's a little bit funny this feeling inside<br>I'm not one of those who can easily hide<br>I don't have much money but boy if I did<br>I'd buy a big house where we both could live<br><br>If I was a sculptor, oh, but then again, no<br>Or a man who makes potions in a travelling show<br>I know it's not much but it's the best I can do<br>My gift is my song and this one's for you<br><br>And you can tell everybody this is your song<br>It may be quite simple but now that it's done<br>I hope you don't mind<br>I hope you don't mind that I put down in words<br>How wonderful life is while you're in the world</i>
</b><br><br>I seriously think its the perfect song for Camryn and Andrew. I really imagine him singing this song to Camryn and it melts my insides.. I feel extremely giddy just thinking about it.<br><br>Oh and last but not the least can I just say...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384052425ra/6757087.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seriously. Andrew is a total keeper! If I meet someone like him, I'd really throw my underwear across the room!! :D LOL. Just kidding!<br><br>All in all. I am totally in love with this book! This book left a mark on me and I will really really treasure it forever!<br><br><b>Amazing job JA Redmerski!!</b><br>**************<br><b>Holy Smokes! Best ending ever in the entire universe!!!<br>That was seriously AMAZING!</b><br><br>Right now I'm...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383736604ra/6649173.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To read an excerpt and join the giveaway for a print <b>COPY</b> of the Edge of Always. Check out the link below!! :)<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://sweetandsexybookreviews.blogspot.com/2013/11/super-sweet-giveaway-edge-of-always.html">http://sweetandsexybookreviews.blogsp...</a><br><br>My long and heartfelt review to follow!!<br><br>*sob*<br><br>*sob*<br><br><b>Oh Andrew!!</b></span>

<div id="review_536470122" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/536470122" />
    <a title="Georgia Cruz" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8816126-georgia-cruz"><img alt="Georgia Cruz" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1454052223p2/8816126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/536470122?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Georgia Cruz" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Georgia Cruz" href="/user/show/8816126-georgia-cruz">Georgia Cruz</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17374029-the-edge-of-always">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8816126-georgia-cruz?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8816126-georgia-cruz?shelf=best-book-ever">best-book-ever</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8816126-georgia-cruz?shelf=best-of-best-books-ever">best-of-best-books-ever</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8816126-georgia-cruz?shelf=will-forever-haunt-me">will-forever-haunt-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8816126-georgia-cruz?shelf=book-boyfriend-list">book-boyfriend-list</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8816126-georgia-cruz?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer536470122" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2870718620651847953"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Our story is over, yes, but our journey isn't, because we'll always live on the edge until the day we die."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>OH. MY. GOD! ANDREW PARRISH = Perfect. Man. *sigh*<br/><br/><b>Andrew & Camryn takes us once again to another journey of their lives into a whole new level!</b> After experiencing loss and “moment of weakness”, Andrew will take another risk to get Camryn back to where they belong: On the road. (of course the Chevelle is taking another trip of a lifetime with them!)<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"Because this is our life. </i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText2870718620651847953" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Our story is over, yes, but our journey isn't, because we'll always live on the edge until the day we die."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />OH. MY. GOD! ANDREW PARRISH = Perfect. Man. *sigh*<br /><br /><b>Andrew &amp; Camryn takes us once again to another journey of their lives into a whole new level!</b> After experiencing loss and “moment of weakness”, Andrew will take another risk to get Camryn back to where they belong: On the road. (of course the Chevelle is taking another trip of a lifetime with them!)<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>"Because this is our life. We met on the road; we grew to know and to love each other on the road. It's where we were meant to be for however long, and it's what we're going to do until it becomes clear that we were meant to do something else."</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />And in this second book, it’s gonna be more fun, drama, full of sexy perverted antics from Andrew, swoonfest moments and lots of surprises they will encounter while on the road. They will make more greatest memories; will again experience the living in the now, and <u>to prove that spontaneity is more rewarding than a meticulously planned life.</u><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“There’s nothing either of us can do to avoid it or to hold it off. All we can control is how we live our lives before it comes for us. So let’s promise each other things that we can hold true to no matter what.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />It’s not really all about Andrew’s POVs, but Redmerski made POVs for both of them. Another thing I really love about this series is that once you started it, YOU. CAN’T. PUT. IT. DOWN. I was deprived from sleep but it’s totally worth the read! If only I could put 10 more stars, that’s how beautiful this series is. <br /><br />I cried for like forever, especially when they made their vows in their wedding day! I can’t put it right here cause it’ll spoil many readers, so let’s just say that I <i>sort of</i> bawled like a baby because they are really deep and it makes me wanna worship them! Even their vows are spontaneous and that is really amazing! God, it’s so beautiful and makes my heart melt! <br />Here’s a little peek of what they had promised to one another:<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“… I promise that if you ever forget me, I’ll read to you like Noah read to Allie..”<br />“… I promise to love you forever in this life and wherever we go in the afterlife, because I know I can’t go on in any life unless you’re in it too.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />I wish there’s an Andrew Parrish in real life! I’ll combed the universe to find him. I truly adore this fictional character! If only I can grab him inside my kindle! Lol<br /><br /><br /> 			 *********************<br /><b>This series taught me a lot of things: To live life the fullest, never regret the decision you made, to never take a second of it for granted because any second could be your last, to be free-spirited and driven and in love with the World. The things that Andrew &amp; Camryn went through together, I can’t help but be awed by them. They inspire me and how I wish in the future, I can do those things they did around the world.</b><br /><br /><br /><b>J.A Redmerski really did a stunning series and I’m still tearing up to pieces because I’m going to miss Andrew &amp; Camryn so much. Hands down to this amazing author! Cant wait for your next books to come!</b><br /><br />And lastly, I once again (just like I did in the first book) dedicate this song for this series because it’s the one that’s been playing on my mind while reading Andrew &amp; Camryn’s journey:<br /><br /><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=sxHWomxc1WQ" rel="nofollow noopener">"Glowing" by The Script</a><br /><blockquote>You knocked me sideways<br />When you said that you were leaving.<br />You knocked me over<br />When you cried and told the truth.<br />And you left me speechless<br />The secrets you've been keeping<br />You're running now, 'cause someone's chasing you<br /><br />And you bought a ticket<br />But you don't know where you're going<br />And you won't tell me<br />For fear I'll follow suit<br />And you're tryin' to save me<br />From your past of bad decisions<br />But my decision's always gonna be<br />To follow you (to follow you)<br /><br />Never gonna stop 'til the clock stops tickin'<br />Never gonna quit 'til my legs stop kickin'<br />I will follow you and we'll both go missin'<br />No I'm never givin' up 'til my heart stops beatin'<br />Never lettin' go 'til my lungs stop breathing<br />I will follow you and we'll both go missin'<br /><br />No, I and we don't even know where we're going<br />But I'm sitting with you and I'm glowing.</blockquote><br /><br /><i>*ARC PROVIDED BY NETGALLEY! Thank you so much!*</i><br /><br />Oh! This is the Gunne Sax vintage dress I pictured on Cam's wedding:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://buildlicious.com/bohemian-wedding-dresses-for-sale/sale-today-only-vintage-gunne-sax-bohemian-wedding-by-bowinston/">http://buildlicious.com/bohemian-wedd...</a></span>

<div id="review_536705169" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/536705169" />
    <a title="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14351108-deanna-pink-lady"><img alt="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1370640721p2/14351108.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/536705169?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" href="/user/show/14351108-deanna-pink-lady">Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17374029-the-edge-of-always">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer536705169" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8255410337609931785"><i>4 "Unconditional Love" Stars</i><br/><br/><b>When everything falls apart, love remains...</b><br/><br/>This is the continuation of the love story of Andrew and Camryn. After all that was endured in The Edge of Never, isn't it time for their HEA? Nothing in life is a certainty and Andrew and Camryn find that out the hard way. They are tested and when that happens, Andrew decides what must be done....<br/><b>We met on the road; we grew to know and to love each other on the road. It's where we were meant to be for however long, and it's</b></span>
  <span id="freeText8255410337609931785" style="display:none"><i>4 "Unconditional Love" Stars</i><br><br><b>When everything falls apart, love remains...</b><br><br>This is the continuation of the love story of Andrew and Camryn. After all that was endured in The Edge of Never, isn't it time for their HEA? Nothing in life is a certainty and Andrew and Camryn find that out the hard way. They are tested and when that happens, Andrew decides what must be done....<br><b>We met on the road; we grew to know and to love each other on the road. It's where we were meant to be for however long, and it's what we're going to do until it becomes clear that we were meant to do something else.</b>.....and so we go on their journey again, to the place that brought them together.<br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/ANDREW_zps93c96e96.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384297882i/6840698._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo ANDREW_zps93c96e96.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>"I want you to stay strong and not let your fear of the past taint the path to our future."</b><br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/camryn_zps04bf5a50.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384297882i/6840699._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo camryn_zps04bf5a50.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Their story is one of <i>UNCONDITIONAL LOVE</i>. It's beautiful, sweet, romantic, sexy and down right perfection. Andrew is what every girl should have in their life. <br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/TEOA2_zpsc5155f1b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384297882i/6840700._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo TEOA2_zpsc5155f1b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I loved the beginning and then I will have to say that I found it a little slow in the middle. Then once I got to the last 3rd, I fell back in love with the book. Their love was always present and beautiful, it just may have been too sweet in the middle. I hate to say that because it is truly a Wonderful, Unconditional Love Story.<br><br>The epilogue was fabulous. I loved the time frame it covered and the ending for me was PERFECTION, just like Andrew and Camryn.<br><br>In closing, I would like to think of them singing this by their favorite group- The Civil Wars<br>Dance Me to the End of Love<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Y9s4y9eK-Hg">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Y9s4y9...</a><br><br>and of course their signature song- Barton Hollow<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=XFlRxMJPM_0">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=XFlRxM...</a><br><br>BR with Barb, Jxxx, and Aimie!! ♥♥♥<br> <br><br></span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('jacgF7K83agukW4slrem24kc5p8fLwmM1Xq0iHVMCheeWRBF6s6uW14a1WnI+fnl083vzbfh7fdez1Abvge+Rw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('621BWzLEFQYOQHLiLT81R92C3yHfd7DKWjdyccTfL074k3EJarZm9X7LyadzcWp5h1PWc3e5VLHRgpbiD5SbHg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer16781600532464420776">J.A. (Jessica) Redmerski is a <i>New York Times</i>, <i>USA Today,</i> and <i>Wall Street Journal</i> bestselling author, international bestseller, and award winner, who juggles several different genres. She began self-publishing in 2012, and later with the success of THE EDGE OF NEVER, signed on with Grand Central Publishing/Forever Romance. Her works have been translated into more than twenty languages.<br/><br/>Jessica is a </span>
  <span id="freeText16781600532464420776" style="display:none">J.A. (Jessica) Redmerski is a <i>New York Times</i>, <i>USA Today,</i> and <i>Wall Street Journal</i> bestselling author, international bestseller, and award winner, who juggles several different genres. She began self-publishing in 2012, and later with the success of THE EDGE OF NEVER, signed on with Grand Central Publishing/Forever Romance. Her works have been translated into more than twenty languages.<br /><br />Jessica is a hybrid author who, in addition to working with a traditional publisher, also continues to self-publish. Her popular crime and suspense series, <i>In the Company of Killers</i>, has been optioned for television and film by actor and model William Levy.<br /><br />What book is Jessica most proud to have written? It's a question she gets asked often. The answer is, hands down, DIRTY EDEN. <i>"DIRTY EDEN was an entirely organic experience for me, as was the story from beginning to end; nothing was planned, and I didn't know the end myself until I got there. As much as I enjoy writing love stories and crime novels, a big part of my heart really does lie in the satirical and strange. I just wish more people would read it."</i><br /><br />What book is Jessica most proud to have written? It's a question she gets asked quite often. The answer is, hands down, DIRTY EDEN. <i>"DIRTY EDEN was an entirely organic experience for me, as was the story from beginning to end; nothing was planned, and I didn't know the end myself until I got there. As much as I enjoy writing love stories and crime novels, a big part of my heart really does lie in the satirical and strange. I just wish more people would read it."</i></span>
